–í–æ—Ç —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ —á—É–≤–∞–∫–∞ —Å —Ä–µ–¥–∏—Ç–∞:
edited 3 months ago
Hi everybody, I have tested some IKEA bulbs on Chinese region with a newest Xiaomi Home app. I would like to share with you which bulbs are working properly and which is NOT so you don't need to waste your time and money to try it. Some info from an another user from Hungarian MIUI forum. (especially thanks for Zoli50)

WORKING

IKEA TRADFRI bulb E27 Cold/Warm white 980lm 2700K 12kWh/1000h Dimmed IKEA product number: 703.389.32

IKEA TRADFRI bulb E14 Warm white 400lm 2700K 5,3kWh/1000h Dimmed IKEA product number: 603.652.71

Yeelight Smart LED Bulb (Color) E27 smart Xiaomi Shop product number: 1251

NOT WORKING

A) - IKEA TRADFRI bulb E27 Warm white 1000lm 2700K 13kWh/1000h Dimmed IKEA product number: 603.652.71

B) - IKEA TRADFRI bulb E27 Cold/Warm white/color RGB 600lm 2700K 8.6kWh/1000h IKEA product number: 004.086.12

C) - Xiaomi/Philips WiFi Bulb E27 White Model: 9290020093

D) - Xiaomi Mi LED Smart Bulb (Color) E27 smart Model: MJDP02YL

I hope it is help, please continue this list with your experience, we should move this info closer. :)

Additionaly, I need the community help as well. I could share the first bulb with my partner but I can not share the new ones. I am not able to share bulbs anymore because the share button is grey, not available anymore. We are on the same region and we use Xiaomi Mijia Gateway. I could shared the first but now it is grey for the first bulb as well. Please give me suggestions how can I solve this issue. Thanks in advance, Have a great day!
